***ะฒะธะบัะพัะธะฝะฐ.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ะฒะธะบัะพัะธะฝะฐ.html>ะฒะธะบัะพัะธฬะฝะฐ</a> (30582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First appeared in the Russian magazine <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ogoniok" class="extiw" title="w:Ogoniok">Ogoniok</a> in 1928. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mikhail_Koltsov" class="extiw" title="w:Mikhail Koltsov">Mikhail Koltsov</a>, the magazine's founder, applied the term to a selection of puzzles in the magazine. He had named the feature after a fellow employee who prepared the feature, <b>Viktor</b> Mikul<b>in</b> (<b>ะะธะบัะพั</b> ะะธะบัะป<b>ะธะฝ</b>).
</p>
